  4583	RZ_IPI bool rz_core_analysis_function_set_signature(RzCore *core, RzAnalysisFunction *fcn, const char *newsig) {
  4584	        bool res = false;
  4585	        char *fcnname = NULL;
  4586	        char *fcnstr = rz_str_newf("%s;", newsig);
  4587	        char *fcnstr_copy = rz_str_dup(fcnstr);
  4588	        char *fcnname_aux = strtok(fcnstr_copy, "(");
  4589	        if (!fcnname_aux) {
  4590	                goto err;
  4591	        }
  4592	        rz_str_trim_tail(fcnname_aux);
  4593	        const char *ls = rz_str_lchr(fcnname_aux, ' ');
  4594	        fcnname = rz_str_dup(ls ? ls : fcnname_aux);
  4595	        if (!fcnname) {
  4596	                goto err;
  4597	        }
  4598	        // TODO: move this into rz_analysis_function_set_type_str()
  4599	        if (strcmp(fcn->name, fcnname)) {
  4600	                (void)rz_core_analysis_function_rename(core, fcn->addr, fcnname);
  4601	                fcn = rz_analysis_get_fcn_in(core->analysis, fcn->addr, -1);
  4602	        }
  4603	        rz_analysis_function_set_type_str(core->analysis, fcn, fcnstr);
  4604	        res = true;
  4605	err:
  4606	        free(fcnname);
  4607	        free(fcnstr_copy);
  4608	        free(fcnstr);
  4609	        return res;
  4610	}

  4656	static void cb_in_range_aav(RzCore *core, ut64 from, ut64 to, int vsize, void *user) {
  4657	        int arch_align = rz_analysis_archinfo(core->analysis, RZ_ANALYSIS_ARCHINFO_TEXT_ALIGN);
  4658	        bool vinfun = rz_config_get_b(core->config, "analysis.vinfun");
  4659	        int searchAlign = rz_config_get_i(core->config, "search.align");
  4660	        int align = (arch_align < 1) ? searchAlign : arch_align;
  4661	        if (arch_align < 0 || (!aligns(from, align) || !aligns(to, align))) {
  4662	                // If archaling < 0, the arch has no alignment defined. Hence it is
  4663	                // ignored if isFine stays false.
  4664	                bool itsFine = false;
  4665	                if (archIsThumbable(core)) {
  4666	                        if ((from & 1) || (to & 1)) {
  4667	                                itsFine = true;
  4668	                        }
  4669	                }
  4670	                if (!itsFine) {
  4671	                        return;
  4672	                }
  4673	                RZ_LOG_DEBUG("Warning: aav: false positive in 0x%08" PFMT64x "\n", from);
  4674	        }
  4675	        if (!vinfun) {
  4676	                RzAnalysisFunction *fcn = rz_analysis_get_fcn_in(core->analysis, from, -1);
  4677	                if (fcn) {
  4678	                        return;
  4679	                }
  4680	        }
  4681	
  4682	        rz_analysis_xrefs_set(core->analysis, from, to, RZ_ANALYSIS_XREF_TYPE_NULL);
  4683	        rz_meta_set(core->analysis, RZ_META_TYPE_DATA, from, vsize, NULL);
  4684	        if (!rz_flag_get_at(core->flags, to, false)) {
  4685	                char *name = rz_str_newf("aav.0x%08" PFMT64x, to);
  4686	                rz_flag_set(core->flags, name, to, vsize);
  4687	                free(name);
  4688	        }
  4689	}

  2748	/**
  2749	 * Print stackpointer info between offset and disassembly like
  2750	 *     0x08049413   -12 -= 4       push  str.echoes
  2751	 */
  2752	static void ds_print_stackptr(RzDisasmState *ds) {
  2753	        if (!ds->show_stackptr) {
  2754	                return;
  2755	        }
  2756	        RzStackAddr sp = ds_stackptr_at(ds, ds->at);
  2757	        if (sp == RZ_STACK_ADDR_INVALID) {
  2758	                rz_cons_print("    ? ");
  2759	        } else {
  2760	                rz_cons_printf("%5" PFMT64d " ", sp);
  2761	        }
  2762	        char *eff = rz_analysis_op_describe_sp_effect(&ds->analysis_op);
  2763	        if (eff) {
  2764	                rz_cons_print(eff);
  2765	                int len = strlen(eff);
  2766	                for (; len < 6; len++) {
  2767	                        rz_cons_print(" ");
  2768	                }
  2769	        } else {
  2770	                rz_cons_print("      ");
  2771	        }
  2772	}

  2883	                rz_analysis_xrefs_set(core->analysis, xref_from, xref_to, RZ_ANALYSIS_XREF_TYPE_DATA);
  2884	                rz_name_filter(string, -1, true);
  2885	                char *flagname = rz_str_newf("str.%s", string);
  2886	                rz_flag_space_push(core->flags, RZ_FLAGS_FS_STRINGS);
  2887	                rz_flag_set(core->flags, flagname, xref_to, length);
  2888	                rz_flag_space_pop(core->flags);
  2889	                rz_meta_set_with_subtype(core->analysis, RZ_META_TYPE_STRING, encoding, xref_to, length, string);
  2890	                free(string);
  2891	                free(flagname);
  2892	        }
  2893	}
  2894	
  2895	static inline bool aligns(ut64 addr, size_t align) {
  2896	        return align > 0 && addr % align == 0;
  2897	}
  2898	
  2899	static void cb_in_range_aav(RzCore *core, ut64 from, ut64 to, int vsize, void *user);
  2900	
  2901	RZ_API int rz_core_search_value_in_range(RzCore *core, RzInterval search_itv, ut64 vmin,
  2902	        ut64 vmax, int vsize, inRangeCb cb, void *cb_user) {
  2903	        int i, align = core->search->align, hitctr = 0;
  2904	        bool vinfun = rz_config_get_b(core->config, "analysis.vinfun");
  2905	        bool vinfunr = rz_config_get_b(core->config, "analysis.vinfunrange");
  2906	        bool analyze_strings = rz_config_get_b(core->config, "analysis.strings");
  2907	        bool big_endian = rz_config_get_b(core->config, "cfg.bigendian");
  2908	        ut8 buf[4096];
  2909	        ut64 v64, value = 0, size;
  2910	        ut64 from = rz_itv_begin(search_itv), to = rz_itv_end(search_itv);
  2911	        ut32 v32;
  2912	        ut16 v16;
  2913	        if (from >= to) {
  2914	                RZ_LOG_ERROR("core: `from` must be lower than `to`\n");
  2915	                return -1;
  2916	        }
  2917	        bool maybeThumb = false;
  2918	        if (align > 1 && core->analysis->cur && core->analysis->cur->arch) {
  2919	                if (!strcmp(core->analysis->cur->arch, "arm") && core->analysis->bits != 64) {
  2920	                        maybeThumb = true;
  2921	                }
  2922	        }
  2923	
  2924	        if (vmin >= vmax) {
  2925	                RZ_LOG_ERROR("core: `vmin` must be lower than `vmax`\n");
  2926	                return -1;
  2927	        }
  2928	        if (to == UT64_MAX) {
  2929	                RZ_LOG_ERROR("core: invalid destination boundary\n");
  2930	                return -1;
  2931	        }
  2932	        rz_cons_break_push(NULL, NULL);
  2933	
  2934	        if (!rz_io_is_valid_offset(core->io, from, 0)) {
  2935	                hitctr = -1;
  2936	                goto beach;
  2937	        }
  2938	        while (from < to) {
  2939	                size = RZ_MIN(to - from, sizeof(buf));
  2940	                memset(buf, 0xff, sizeof(buf)); // probably unnecessary
  2941	                if (rz_cons_is_breaked()) {
  2942	                        goto beach;
  2943	                }
  2944	                bool res = rz_io_read_at_mapped(core->io, from, buf, size);
  2945	                if (!res || !memcmp(buf, "\xff\xff\xff\xff", 4) || !memcmp(buf, "\x00\x00\x00\x00", 4)) {
  2946	                        if (!isValidAddress(core, from)) {
  2947	                                ut64 next = rz_io_map_next_address(core->io, from);
  2948	                                if (next == UT64_MAX) {
  2949	                                        from += sizeof(buf);
  2950	                                } else {
  2951	                                        from += (next - from);
  2952	                                }
  2953	                                continue;
  2954	                        }
  2955	                }
  2956	                if (size <= vsize) {
  2957	                        break;
  2958	                }
  2959	                RzAnalysisOp *op = rz_analysis_op_new();
  2960	                for (i = 0; i <= (size - vsize); i++) {
  2961	                        void *v = (buf + i);
  2962	                        ut64 addr = from + i;
  2963	                        if (rz_cons_is_breaked()) {
  2964	                                rz_analysis_op_free(op);
  2965	                                goto beach;
  2966	                        }
  2967	                        if (!aligns(addr, align)) {
  2968	                                continue;
  2969	                        }
  2970	                        int match = false;
  2971	                        int left = size - i;
  2972	                        if (vsize > left) {
  2973	                                break;
  2974	                        }
  2975	                        switch (vsize) {
  2976	                        case 1:
  2977	                                value = rz_read_ble8(v);
  2978	                                match = (buf[i] >= vmin && buf[i] <= vmax);
  2979	                                break;
  2980	                        case 2:
  2981	                                v16 = rz_read_ble16(v, big_endian);
  2982	                                match = (v16 >= vmin && v16 <= vmax);
  2983	                                value = v16;
  2984	                                break;
  2985	                        case 4:
  2986	                                v32 = rz_read_ble32(v, big_endian);
  2987	                                match = (v32 >= vmin && v32 <= vmax);
  2988	                                value = v32;
  2989	                                break;
  2990	                        case 8:
  2991	                                v64 = rz_read_ble64(v, big_endian);
  2992	                                match = (v64 >= vmin && v64 <= vmax);
  2993	                                value = v64;
  2994	                                break;
  2995	                        default:
  2996	                                RZ_LOG_ERROR("core: unknown vsize %d (supported only 1,2,4,8)\n", vsize);
  2997	                                hitctr = -1;
  2998	                                rz_analysis_op_free(op);
  2999	                                goto beach;
  3000	                        }
  3001	                        if (match && !vinfun) {
  3002	                                if (vinfunr) {
  3003	                                        if (rz_analysis_get_fcn_in_bounds(core->analysis, addr, RZ_ANALYSIS_FCN_TYPE_NULL)) {
  3004	                                                match = false;
  3005	                                        }
  3006	                                } else {
  3007	                                        if (rz_analysis_get_fcn_in(core->analysis, addr, RZ_ANALYSIS_FCN_TYPE_NULL)) {
  3008	                                                match = false;
  3009	                                        }
  3010	                                }
  3011	                        }
  3012	                        if (match && value) {
  3013	                                bool isValidMatch = true;
  3014	                                if (!aligns(value, align)) {
  3015	                                        // ignored .. unless we are analyzing arm/thumb and lower bit is 1
  3016	                                        isValidMatch = false;
  3017	                                        if (maybeThumb && (value & 1)) {
  3018	                                                isValidMatch = true;
  3019	                                        }
  3020	                                }
  3021	                                if (isValidMatch) {
  3022	                                        cb(core, addr, value, vsize, cb_user);
  3023	                                        if (analyze_strings) {
  3024	                                                rz_core_add_string_ref(core, addr, value);
  3025	                                        }
  3026	                                        hitctr++;
  3027	                                }
  3028	                        }
  3029	                        if (!match && core->analysis && op && cb == cb_in_range_aav) {
  3030	                                rz_analysis_op_init(op);
  3031	                                int oplen = rz_analysis_op(core->analysis, op, from + i, buf + i, vsize, RZ_ANALYSIS_OP_MASK_BASIC);
  3032	                                if (oplen > 0) {
  3033	                                        i += oplen - 1;
  3034	                                }
  3035	                                rz_analysis_op_fini(op);
  3036	                        }
  3037	                }
  3038	                rz_analysis_op_free(op);
  3039	                if (size == to - from) {
  3040	                        break;
  3041	                }
  3042	                from += size - vsize + 1;
  3043	        }
  3044	beach:
  3045	        rz_cons_break_pop();
  3046	        return hitctr;
  3047	}
  3048

  3050	        HtUU *visited;
  3051	        RzList /*<RzAnalysisBlock *>*/ *path;
  3052	        RzCore *core;
  3053	        ut64 from;
  3054	        RzAnalysisBlock *fromBB;
  3055	        ut64 to;

   404	                if (space) {

   411	        ut64 min_space_i = n_spaces + 1;
   412	        rz_list_foreach (list, iter, flg) {
   413	                // get the "priority" of the flag flagspace and
   414	                // check if better than what we found so far
   415	                for (i = 0; i < n_spaces; i++) {
   416	                        if (flg->space == spaces[i]) {

   440	        return (!strncmp(n, "sym.func.", 9) || !strncmp(n, "method.", 7) || !strncmp(n, "sym.", 4) || !strncmp(n, "func.", 5) || !strncmp(n, "fcn.0", 5));
   441	}
   442	
   443	/* returns the last flag item defined before or at the given offset.
   444	 * NULL is returned if such a item is not found. */
   445	RZ_API RzFlagItem *rz_flag_get_at(RzFlag *f, ut64 off, bool closest) {
   446	        rz_return_val_if_fail(f, NULL);
   447	
   448	        RzFlagItem *nice = NULL;
   449	        RzListIter *iter;
   450	        const RzFlagsAtOffset *flags_at = rz_flag_get_nearest_list(f, off, -1);
   451	        if (!flags_at) {
   452	                return NULL;
   453	        }
   454	        if (flags_at->off == off) {
   455	                RzFlagItem *item;
   456	                rz_list_foreach (flags_at->flags, iter, item) {
   457	                        if (IS_FI_NOTIN_SPACE(f, item)) {
   458	                                continue;
   459	                        }
   460	                        if (nice) {
   461	                                if (isFunctionFlag(nice->name)) {
   462	                                        nice = item;
   463	                                }
   464	                        } else {
   465	                                nice = item;
   466	                        }
   467	                }
   468	                if (nice) {
   469	                        return evalFlag(f, nice);
   470	                }
   471	        }
   472	
   473	        if (!closest) {
   474	                return NULL;
   475	        }

    10	// for map perms
    11	RZ_API bool rz_io_addr_is_mapped(RzIO *io, ut64 vaddr) {
    12	        rz_return_val_if_fail(io, false);
    13	        return (io->va && rz_io_map_get(io, vaddr));
    14	}
    15	
    16	// when io.va is true this checks if the highest priorized map at this
    17	// offset has the same or high permissions set. When there is no map it
    18	// check for the current desc permissions and size.
    19	// when io.va is false it only checks for the desc
    20	RZ_API bool rz_io_is_valid_offset(RzIO *io, ut64 offset, int hasperm) {
    21	        rz_return_val_if_fail(io, false);
    22	        if (io->va) {
    23	                if (!hasperm) {
    24	                        // return rz_io_map_is_mapped (io, offset);
    25	                        RzIOMap *map = rz_io_map_get(io, offset);
    26	                        return map ? map->perm & RZ_PERM_R : false;
    27	                }
    28	                RzIOMap *map = rz_io_map_get(io, offset);
    29	                return map ? (map->perm & hasperm) == hasperm : false;
    30	        }

    32	                return false;
    33	        }
    34	        if (offset > rz_io_desc_size(io->desc)) {
    35	                return false;
    36	        }

static bool aav_refptr_has_flag(RzCore *core, ut64 addr, int vsize) {$
        if (!core || !core->io || !core->flags || (vsize != 1 && vsize != 2 && vsize != 4 && vsize != 8)) {$
                return false;$
        }$
        ut64 refptr = UT64_MAX;$
        bool big_endian = rz_config_get_b(core->config, "cfg.bigendian");$
        if (!rz_io_read_i(core->io, addr, &refptr, vsize, big_endian) || !refptr || refptr == UT64_MAX) {$
                return false;$
        }$
        return rz_flag_get_i(core->flags, refptr) != NULL;$
}$
$
static void cb_in_range_aav(RzCore *core, ut64 from, ut64 to, int vsize, void *user) {$
        int arch_align = rz_analysis_archinfo(core->analysis, RZ_ANALYSIS_ARCHINFO_TEXT_ALIGN);$
        bool vinfun = rz_config_get_b(core->config, "analysis.vinfun");$
        int searchAlign = rz_config_get_i(core->config, "search.align");$
        int align = (arch_align < 1) ? searchAlign : arch_align;$
        if (arch_align < 0 || (!aligns(from, align) || !aligns(to, align))) {$
                // If archaling < 0, the arch has no alignment defined. Hence it is$
                // ignored if isFine stays false.$
                bool itsFine = false;$
                if (archIsThumbable(core)) {$
                        if ((from & 1) || (to & 1)) {$
                                itsFine = true;$
                        }$
                }$
                if (!itsFine) {$
                        return;$
                }$
                RZ_LOG_DEBUG("Warning: aav: false positive in 0x%08" PFMT64x "\n", from);$
        }$
        if (!vinfun) {$
                RzAnalysisFunction *fcn = rz_analysis_get_fcn_in(core->analysis, from, -1);$
                if (fcn) {$
                        return;$
                }$
        }$
$
        rz_analysis_xrefs_set(core->analysis, from, to, RZ_ANALYSIS_XREF_TYPE_NULL);$
        rz_meta_set(core->analysis, RZ_META_TYPE_DATA, from, vsize, NULL);$
        if (rz_flag_get_at(core->flags, to, false) || aav_refptr_has_flag(core, to, vsize)) {$
                return;$
        }$
        char *name = rz_str_newf("aav.0x%08" PFMT64x, to);$
        rz_flag_set(core->flags, name, to, vsize);$
        free(name);$

+        ut64 types = 0;
+        RzRegSet *rs = NULL;
+        if (!core) {
+                return 0;
+        }
+        rs = rz_reg_regset_get(core->analysis->reg, RZ_REG_TYPE_GPR);
+        if (rs) {
+                RzRegItem *r;
+                RzListIter *iter;
+                rz_list_foreach (rs->regs, iter, r) {
+                        if (r->type == RZ_REG_TYPE_GPR) {
+                                ut64 val = rz_reg_getv(core->analysis->reg, r->name);
+                                if (addr == val) {
+                                        types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_REG;
+                                        break;
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+        if (rz_flag_get_i(core->flags, addr)) {
+                types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_FLAG;
+        }
+        if (rz_analysis_get_fcn_in(core->analysis, addr, 0)) {
+                types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_FUNC;
+        }
+        // check registers
+        if (rz_core_is_debug(core)) {
+                RzDebugMap *map;
+                RzListIter *iter;
+                // use 'dm'
+                // XXX: this line makes rz debugging MUCH slower
+                // rz_debug_map_sync (core->dbg);
+                rz_list_foreach (core->dbg->maps, iter, map) {
+                        if (addr >= map->addr && addr < map->addr_end) {
+                                if (map->name && map->name[0] == '/') {
+                                        if (core->io && core->io->desc &&
+                                                core->io->desc->name &&
+                                                !strcmp(map->name,
+                                                        core->io->desc->name)) {
+                                                types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_PROGRAM;
+                                        } else {
+                                                types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_LIBRARY;
+                                        }
+                                }
+                                if (map->perm & RZ_PERM_X) {
+                                        types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_EXEC;
+                                }
+                                if (map->perm & RZ_PERM_R) {
+                                        types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_READ;
+                                }
+                                if (map->perm & RZ_PERM_W) {
+                                        types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_WRITE;
+                                }
+                                // find function
+                                if (map->name && strstr(map->name, "heap")) {
+                                        types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_HEAP;
+                                }
+                                if (map->name && strstr(map->name, "stack")) {
+                                        types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_STACK;
+                                }
+                                break;
+                        }
+                }
+        } else {
+                int _perm = -1;
+                if (core->io) {
+                        // sections
+                        void **it;
+                        RzPVector *maps = rz_io_maps(core->io);
+                        rz_pvector_foreach (maps, it) {
+                                RzIOMap *s = *it;
+                                if (addr >= s->itv.addr && addr < (s->itv.addr + s->itv.size)) {
+                                        // sections overlap, so we want to get the one with lower perms
+                                        _perm = (_perm != -1) ? RZ_MIN(_perm, s->perm) : s->perm;
+                                        // TODO: we should identify which maps come from the program or other
+                                        // types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_PROGRAM;
+                                        // find function those sections should be created by hand or esil init
+                                        if (s->name && strstr(s->name, "heap")) {
+                                                types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_HEAP;
+                                        }
+                                        if (s->name && strstr(s->name, "stack")) {
+                                                types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_STACK;
+                                        }
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+                if (_perm != -1) {
+                        if (_perm & RZ_PERM_X) {
+                                types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_EXEC;
+                        }
+                        if (_perm & RZ_PERM_R) {
+                                types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_READ;
+                        }
+                        if (_perm & RZ_PERM_W) {
+                                types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_WRITE;
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        // check if it's ascii
+        if (addr != 0) {
+                int not_ascii = 0;
+                int i, failed_sequence, dir, on;
+                for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
+                        ut8 n = (addr >> (i * 8)) & 0xff;
+                        if (n && !IS_PRINTABLE(n)) {
+                                not_ascii = 1;
+                        }
+                }
+                if (!not_ascii) {
+                        types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_ASCII;
+                }
+                failed_sequence = 0;
+                dir = on = -1;
+                for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
+                        ut8 n = (addr >> (i * 8)) & 0xff;
+                        if (on != -1) {
+                                if (dir == -1) {
+                                        dir = (n > on) ? 1 : -1;
+                                }
+                                if (n == on + dir) {
+                                        // ok
+                                } else {
+                                        failed_sequence = 1;
+                                        break;
+                                }
+                        }
+                        on = n;
+                }
+                if (!failed_sequence) {
+                        types |= RZ_ANALYSIS_ADDR_TYPE_SEQUENCE;
+                }
+        }
+        return types;
 }

+                        nameChanged = true;
+                } else if (strncmp(f->name, "sect", 4)) {
+                        rz_analysis_function_rename(fcn, f->name);
+                        nameChanged = true;
+                }
+        }
+        if (!nameChanged) {
+                rz_analysis_function_rename(fcn, rz_strf(tmpbuf, "%s.%08" PFMT64x, fcnpfx, fcn->addr));
+        }
 }

+        return f->space && !strcmp(f->space->name, RZ_FLAGS_FS_SYMBOLS) && rz_str_startswith(f->name, "entry.");
 }
